第五章 词类和词性标注¶

本章目的¶

  • Python
In [1]:
%matplotlib inline
import nltk
from nltk import word_tokenize

词性和词性标注¶

part-of-speech tagger, POS tagger

In [2]:
#
text = word_tokenize("And now for something completely different")
nltk.pos_tag(text)
Out[2]:
[('And', 'CC'),
 ('now', 'RB'),
 ('for', 'IN'),
 ('something', 'NN'),
 ('completely', 'RB'),
 ('different', 'JJ')]
In [3]:
#
text = word_tokenize("They refuse to permit us to obtain the refuse permit")
nltk.pos_tag(text)
Out[3]:
[('They', 'PRP'),
 ('refuse', 'VBP'),
 ('to', 'TO'),
 ('permit', 'VB'),
 ('us', 'PRP'),
 ('to', 'TO'),
 ('obtain', 'VB'),
 ('the', 'DT'),
 ('refuse', 'NN'),
 ('permit', 'NN')]

词性标注器的作用¶

In [4]:
text = nltk.Text(word.lower() for word in nltk.corpus.brown.words())
#woman
text.similar('woman')

man day time year car moment world family house child boy country job
state war way girl place word question
In [5]:
#bought
text.similar('bought')

made done said put seen had found left given heard been got set
brought was that called told felt took
In [6]:
#over
text.similar('over')

in on to of and for with from at by that into as up out down through
is all about
In [7]:
#the
text.similar('the')

a his this their its her an that our any all one these my in your no
some other and

表示已标注的标识符¶

(tagged token)

str2tuple()

In [8]:
tagged_token = nltk.tag.str2tuple('fly/NN')
tagged_token
Out[8]:
('fly', 'NN')
In [9]:
tagged_token[0]
Out[9]:
'fly'

In [10]:
sent =  '''
        The/AT grand/JJ jury/NN commented/VBD on/IN a/AT number/NN of/IN
        other/AP topics/NNS ,/, AMONG/IN them/PPO the/AT Atlanta/NP and/CC
        Fulton/NP-tl County/NN-tl purchasing/VBG departments/NNS which/WDT it/PPS
        said/VBD ``/`` ARE/BER well/QL operated/VBN and/CC follow/VB generally/RB
        accepted/VBN practices/NNS which/WDT inure/VB to/IN the/AT best/JJT
        interest/NN of/IN both/ABX governments/NNS ''/'' ./.
        '''
[nltk.tag.str2tuple(t) for t in sent.split()]
Out[10]:
[('The', 'AT'),
 ('grand', 'JJ'),
 ('jury', 'NN'),
 ('commented', 'VBD'),
 ('on', 'IN'),
 ('a', 'AT'),
 ('number', 'NN'),
 ('of', 'IN'),
 ('other', 'AP'),
 ('topics', 'NNS'),
 (',', ','),
 ('AMONG', 'IN'),
 ('them', 'PPO'),
 ('the', 'AT'),
 ('Atlanta', 'NP'),
 ('and', 'CC'),
 ('Fulton', 'NP-TL'),
 ('County', 'NN-TL'),
 ('purchasing', 'VBG'),
 ('departments', 'NNS'),
 ('which', 'WDT'),
 ('it', 'PPS'),
 ('said', 'VBD'),
 ('``', '``'),
 ('ARE', 'BER'),
 ('well', 'QL'),
 ('operated', 'VBN'),
 ('and', 'CC'),
 ('follow', 'VB'),
 ('generally', 'RB'),
 ('accepted', 'VBN'),
 ('practices', 'NNS'),
 ('which', 'WDT'),
 ('inure', 'VB'),
 ('to', 'IN'),
 ('the', 'AT'),
 ('best', 'JJT'),
 ('interest', 'NN'),
 ('of', 'IN'),
 ('both', 'ABX'),
 ('governments', 'NNS'),
 ("''", "''"),
 ('.', '.')]

读取标注语料库¶

The/at Fulton/np-tl County/nn-tl Grand/jj-tl Jury/nn-tl said/vbd Friday/nr an/at investigation/nn of/in Atlanta's/np$ recent/jj primary/nn election/nn produced/vbd / no/at evidence/nn ''/'' that/cs any/dti irregularities/nns took/vbd place/nn ./.

In [11]:
nltk.corpus.brown.tagged_words()
Out[11]:
[('The', 'AT'), ('Fulton', 'NP-TL'), ...]
In [12]:
print(nltk.corpus.nps_chat.tagged_words())

[('now', 'RB'), ('im', 'PRP'), ('left', 'VBD'), ...]
In [13]:
nltk.corpus.conll2000.tagged_words()
Out[13]:
[('Confidence', 'NN'), ('in', 'IN'), ('the', 'DT'), ...]
In [14]:
nltk.corpus.treebank.tagged_words()
Out[14]:
[('Pierre', 'NNP'), ('Vinken', 'NNP'), (',', ','), ...]
In [15]:
nltk.corpus.brown.tagged_words(tagset='universal')
Out[15]:
[('The', 'DET'), ('Fulton', 'NOUN'), ...]
In [16]:
nltk.corpus.treebank.tagged_words(tagset='universal')
Out[16]:
[('Pierre', 'NOUN'), ('Vinken', 'NOUN'), (',', '.'), ...]
In [17]:
nltk.corpus.sinica_treebank.tagged_words()
Out[17]:
[('', 'Neu'), ('', 'Nad'), ('', 'Nba'), ...]

常见词性¶

In [17]:
from nltk.corpus import brown
brown_news_tagged = brown.tagged_words(categories='news', tagset='universal')
tag_fd = nltk.FreqDist(tag for (word, tag) in brown_news_tagged)
tag_fd.most_common()
Out[17]:
[('NOUN', 30654),
 ('VERB', 14399),
 ('ADP', 12355),
 ('.', 11928),
 ('DET', 11389),
 ('ADJ', 6706),
 ('ADV', 3349),
 ('CONJ', 2717),
 ('PRON', 2535),
 ('PRT', 2264),
 ('NUM', 2166),
 ('X', 92)]
In [18]:
tag_fd.plot(cumulative=True)

名词¶

In [19]:
word_tag_pairs = nltk.bigrams(brown_news_tagged)
noun_preceders = [a[1] for (a, b) in word_tag_pairs if b[1] == 'NOUN']
fdist = nltk.FreqDist(noun_preceders)
[tag for (tag, _) in fdist.most_common()]
Out[19]:
['NOUN',
 'DET',
 'ADJ',
 'ADP',
 '.',
 'VERB',
 'CONJ',
 'NUM',
 'ADV',
 'PRT',
 'PRON',
 'X']

关于词性的条件频率表¶

In [21]:
cfd1 = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist(wsj)
cfd1['yield'].most_common()
Out[21]:
[('VERB', 28), ('NOUN', 20)]
In [22]:
cfd1['cut'].most_common()
Out[22]:
[('VERB', 25), ('NOUN', 3)]

In [23]:
wsj = nltk.corpus.treebank.tagged_words()
cfd2 = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist((tag, word) for (word, tag) in wsj)
list(cfd2['VBN'].most_common())

形容词和副词¶

未简化的标记¶

NN$,SP

-NC-HL-TL

In [27]:
def findtags(tag_prefix, tagged_text):
    cfd = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist((tag, word) for (word, tag) in tagged_text
                                  if tag.startswith(tag_prefix))
    return dict((tag, cfd[tag].most_common(5)) for tag in cfd.conditions())
tagdict = findtags('NN', nltk.corpus.brown.tagged_words(categories='news'))
for tag in sorted(tagdict):
    print(tag, tagdict[tag])

nltk.help.upenn_tagset('JJ')

JJ: adjective or numeral, ordinal
    third ill-mannered pre-war regrettable oiled calamitous first separable
    ectoplasmic battery-powered participatory fourth still-to-be-named
    multilingual multi-disciplinary ...

In [31]:
brown_news_tagged = brown.tagged_words(categories='news', tagset='universal')
data = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist((word.lower(), tag) 
                                for (word, tag) in brown_news_tagged)
for word in sorted(data.conditions()):
    if len(data[word]) > 3:
        tags = [tag for (tag, _) in data[word].most_common()]
        print(word, ' '.join(tags))

利用默认词典处理未登录词¶

nUNK out of vocabulary

In [49]:
alice = nltk.corpus.gutenberg.words('carroll-alice.txt')
vocab = nltk.FreqDist(alice)
v1000 = [word for (word, _) in vocab.most_common(1000)]
mapping = defaultdict(lambda: 'UNK')
for v in v1000:
    mapping[v] = v
alice2 = [mapping[v] for v in alice]
alice2[:100]

words = nltk.corpus.words.words('en')

    key = ''.join(sorted(word))
    anagrams[key].append(word)

正则表达式标注器¶

In [63]:
patterns = [
    (r'.*ing$', 'VBG'),               # gerunds
    (r'.*ed$', 'VBD'),                # simple past
    (r'.*es$', 'VBZ'),                # 3rd singular present
    (r'.*ould$', 'MD'),               # modals
    (r'.*\'s$', 'NN$'),               # possessive nouns
    (r'.*s$', 'NNS'),                 # plural nouns
    (r'^-?[0-9]+(.[0-9]+)?$', 'CD'),  # cardinal numbers
    (r'.*', 'NN')                     # nouns (default)
    ]
regexp_tagger = nltk.RegexpTagger(patterns)
regexp_tagger.tag(brown_sents[3])

查表标注器¶

100UnigramTagger

In [65]:
from nltk.corpus import brown
fd = nltk.FreqDist(brown.words(categories='news'))
cfd = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist(brown.tagged_words(categories='news'))
most_freq_words = fd.most_common(100)
likely_tags = dict((word, cfd[word].max()) for (word, _) in most_freq_words)
baseline_tagger = nltk.UnigramTagger(model=likely_tags)
baseline_tagger.evaluate(brown_tagged_sents)
Out[65]:
0.45578495136941344

查表标注器的性能¶

In [69]:
def performance(cfd, wordlist):
    lt = dict((word, cfd[word].max()) for word in wordlist)
    baseline_tagger = nltk.UnigramTagger(model=lt, backoff=nltk.DefaultTagger('NN'))
    return baseline_tagger.evaluate(brown.tagged_sents(categories='news'))

def display():
    import pylab
    word_freqs = nltk.FreqDist(brown.words(categories='news')).most_common()
    words_by_freq = [w for (w, _) in word_freqs]
    cfd = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist(brown.tagged_words(categories='news'))
    sizes = 2 ** pylab.arange(15)
    perfs = [performance(cfd, words_by_freq[:size]) for size in sizes]
    pylab.plot(sizes, perfs, '-bo')
    pylab.title('Lookup Tagger Performance with Varying Model Size')
    pylab.xlabel('Model Size')
    pylab.ylabel('Performance')
    pylab.show()
display()

性能限制¶

In [80]:
cfd = nltk.ConditionalFreqDist(((x[1], y[1], z[0]), z[1])
            for sent in brown_tagged_sents
            for x, y, z in nltk.trigrams(sent))
ambiguous_contexts = [c for c in cfd.conditions() if len(cfd[c]) > 1]
sum(cfd[c].N() for c in ambiguous_contexts) / cfd.N()
Out[80]:
0.049297702068029296

训练自带的标注器¶

Trigrams'n'Tags

In [82]:
from nltk.corpus import treebank
train_data=treebank.tagged_sents()[:3000]
test_data=treebank.tagged_sents()[3000:]
from nltk.tag import tnt
tnt_pos_tagger=tnt.TnT()
tnt_pos_tagger.train(train_data)
tnt_pos_tagger.evaluate(test_data)
